    <h2>
     <a id="_AndroidMainifestxml_1">
     </a>
     一. AndroidMainifest.xml文件的结构
    </h2>
    <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token prolog">&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;</span>

    package="com.example.tong_xun_lu"&gt;	<span class="token comment">&lt;!--指定appJava程序的包名--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>uses-permission</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>android.permission.CALL_PHONE<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>  <span class="token comment">&lt;!--权限定义--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>application</span>

        android:label="@string/app_name"	<span class="token comment">&lt;!--指明App安装后显示的文字信息--&gt;</span>
        android:theme="@style/Theme.AppCompat.Light.NoActionBar"&gt;	<span class="token comment">&lt;!--指明App的主题风格--&gt;</span>

                <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>category</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>android.intent.category.LAUNCHER<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>	<span class="token comment">&lt;!--决定App是否显示在程序列表里--&gt;</span>
                <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>data</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>mimeType</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>video/mpeq<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>

        <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>activity</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>.addActivity<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>activity</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> <span class="token comment">&lt;!--增加addActivity，注意要加点--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>application</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>manifest</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="_Android_31">
     </a>
     二. Android的四大组件
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Activity_32">
     </a>
     (一) Activity(活动)
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Activity是Android App的表现层，
      <mark>
       显示可视化的用户界面，并且接收与用户交互所产生的界面事件
      </mark>
      ；
      <br/>
      🔰子类Activity需要实现的方法：
      <br/>
      1)
      <code>
       onCreate(Bundle)
      </code>
      ：初始化Activity。使用setContentView(int)方法将布局资源定义到用户界面上；使用findViewById(int)在用户界面中检索需要编程交互的小部件；
      <br/>
      2)
      <code>
       onPause()
      </code>
      ：处理当离开Activity时要做的事情。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_BroadcastReceiver_38">
     </a>
     (二) BroadcastReceiver(广播接收器)
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰BroadcastReceiver是
      <mark>
       用来接收并相应广播消息的组件，他不含任何用户界面，不做任何事情，仅是接受广播并作出相应的反应
      </mark>
      ；
      <br/>
      🔰使用时，可以用Context.registerReceiver()方法在程序代码中动态地注册这个类的使用实例，也可以通过AndroidMainifest.xml中的
      <code>
       &lt;receiver&gt;
      </code>
      标签中静态声明；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Service_42">
     </a>
     (三) Service(服务)
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Service
      <mark>
       没有可视化用户界面，但需要长时间在后台运行的应用
      </mark>
      ；
      <br/>
      🔰使用时，每个Service类在AndroidMainifest.xml中有相应的
      <code>
       &lt;service&gt;
      </code>
      声明；Service可以通过Context.startService()和Context.bindService()启动；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ContentProvider_46">
     </a>
     (四) ContentProvider(内容提供者)
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰 ContentProvider
      <mark>
       是Android提供的一种标准的共享数据机制，App通过它访问其他App私有数据
      </mark>
      ；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="__50">
     </a>
     三. 基础界面组件与布局
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="__51">
     </a>
     (一) 组件共用属性
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性值
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:id=“@+id/tiaoshi”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          ID号
         </mark>
         ，是组件的唯一标识
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_width=“wrap_content”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          组件宽度
         </mark>
         <br/>
         <code>
          wrap_content
         </code>
         :大小适应文本内容
         <br/>
         <code>
          match_parent
         </code>
         :大小适应父组件大小
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_height=“wrap_content”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          组件高度
         </mark>
         <br/>
         <code>
          wrap_content
         </code>
         :大小适应文本内容
         <br/>
         <code>
          match_parent
         </code>
         :大小适应父组件大小
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_weight=“5”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置权重
         </mark>
         ，即让一行或一列的组件按比例显示
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:drawableLeft=“@mipmap/suo”
         <br/>
         android:drawableRight
         <br/>
         android:drawableTop
         <br/>
         android:drawableBottom
        </td>
        <td>
         设置编辑框文本的左边，右边，上边，底部显示的drawable
         <br/>
         <br/>
         如：
         <mark>
          在密码输入框前加个锁
         </mark>
         <img alt="在密码" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/e6f5099fd5a2251485a61f30ec8b5d9b.png"/>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:drawablePadding
        </td>
        <td>
         设置
         <mark>
          编辑框文本与drawable的间隔
         </mark>
         ，与drawableLeft等一起使用，可以设置为负数，单独使用没有效果
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_marginLeft=“30dp”
         <br/>
         android:layout_marginRight
         <br/>
         android:layout_marginTop
         <br/>
         android:layout_marginBottom
        </td>
        <td>
         设置编辑框与手机边缘之间的间距
         <mark>
          (外边距)
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:background=“#369733”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置Image View的
         <mark>
          背景颜色或图片
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_TextView_63">
     </a>
     (二) 文本显示组件【TextView】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       具备基本的显示文本功能，可设置
       <mark>
        文本大小，位置，颜色
       </mark>
       等属性；
      </strong>
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/13b365d10475022358c4edac0fe84f52.png"/>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性值
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:text=“hello world！”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          显示文本内容
         </mark>
         <br/>
         <code>
          btn.setText("你好");
         </code>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:textSize=“20sp”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          文本大小
         </mark>
         ，单位sp
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:textColor=“#973030”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          文本颜色
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:textStyle=“normal”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置字形
         </mark>
         <br/>
         bool 粗体, italic 斜体, normal 正常
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:lines=“2”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置
         <mark>
          文本的行数
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:autoLink=“web”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置是否当文本为：URL链接(all, web)，E-mail(email)，电话号码(phone)，Map(map)时，文本显示可单击的链接
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:gravity=“center”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置文本框内
         <mark>
          文本的对齐方式
         </mark>
         <br/>
         top / bottom / left / right /
         <br/>
         center_horizontal(横向中央位置对齐)
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_gravity=“center”
        </td>
        <td>
         组件本身相对于父组件的显示位置
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Button_77">
     </a>
     (三) 按钮组件【Button】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Button是TextView的子类，所以TextView上的很多属性可以直接应用到Button上；对于Button操作主要是
       <mark>
        按下后执行何种操作
       </mark>
      </strong>
      ；&gt;
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/b03662c403574aa3e7cf9e14f70bf27d.png"/>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:clickable=“true”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置
         <mark>
          是否允许点击按钮
         </mark>
         ，true/false
         <br/>
         <code>
          btn.setClickable(boolean)
         </code>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:background=“#980F0F”
        </td>
        <td>
         通过资源文件
         <mark>
          设置颜色
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:onClick
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置点击事件
         </mark>
         <br/>
         <code>
          setOnClickListener(OnClickListener)
         </code>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__86">
     </a>
     1. 按钮点击监听事件
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java">bt <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Button</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rgWhcd<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
bt<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
     <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
     <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
     <span class="token comment">//	功能代码</span>
     <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_LinearLayout_97">
     </a>
     (四) 线性布局【LinearLayout】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       可以使用
       <mark>
        水平(Horizontal)
       </mark>
       或
       <mark>
        垂直(Vertical)
       </mark>
       两种方式放置组件;
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:orientation=“vertical”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置线性布局的方向
         </mark>
         <br/>
         <code>
          horizontal(水平)
         </code>
         <br/>
         <code>
          vertical(垂直)
         </code>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_EditText_105">
     </a>
     (五) 编辑框组件【EditText】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       EditText是TextView的子类，主要操作是
       <mark>
        用户与AndroidApp进行数据传输的窗口
       </mark>
      </strong>
      ；
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/f8f8d906518c828001a85e2a4822a264.png"/>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:hint=“密码”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置编辑框内容为空时显示的文本
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:inputType=“phone”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置编辑框中限制输入的类型
         </mark>
         ：(number—整数，numberDecimal—小数点，date—日期，text—文本，phone—拨号键盘，textPassword—密码，textVisiblePassword—可见密码，textUri—网址)
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:maxLength=“10”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          限制显示的文本长度
         </mark>
         ，超出部分不显示
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:digits=“123456789”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置允许输入那些字符
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ImageView_115">
     </a>
     (六) 图像显示组件【ImageView】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       用于显示图片，图片可来自资源文件，Drawable对象和ContentProvider
      </strong>
      ;
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:adjustViewBounds=“true”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置Image View是否自动调整边界来适应显示图片的宽长比
         </mark>
         , true/false
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:maxHeight=“20dp”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置Image View的最大高度
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:maxWidth=“20dp”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置Image View的最大宽度
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:scaleType=“matrix”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置Image View所显示的图片如何缩放或移动以适应Image View的大小
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:src=“@mipmap/beijing”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置Image View所显示的图像路径
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰
      <code>
       src
      </code>
      指ImageView上显示的内容，按图片大小填充，不拉伸；
      <code>
       background
      </code>
      指的是背景，会进行拉伸；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_RelativeLayout_127">
     </a>
     (七) 相对布局【RelativeLayout】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       它可以在屏幕大小不同，分辨率不同的Android终端屏幕上友好显示的一种布局方式
      </strong>
      ；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__129">
     </a>
     1. 设置组件与组件之间的关系和位置的相关属性
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        属性名
       </th>
       <th>
        说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_above=“@id/shuru”
       </td>
       <td>
        将
        <mark>
         该组件的底部至于给定的ID组件的上面
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_below=“@id/shuru”
       </td>
       <td>
        将
        <mark>
         该组件的底部至于给定的ID组件的下面
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_toLeftOf=“@id/shuru”
       </td>
       <td>
        将
        <mark>
         该组件的右边缘与给定的ID组件的左边缘对齐
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_toRightOf=“@id/shuru”
       </td>
       <td>
        将
        <mark>
         该组件的左边缘与给定的ID组件的右边缘对齐
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <h4>
     <a id="2__136">
     </a>
     2. 设置组件与组件之间对齐方式的相关属性

    <h4>
     <a id="4__151">
     </a>
     4. 设置组件方向的相关属性
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        属性名
       </th>
       <th>
        说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_centerHoriaontal=“true”
       </td>
       <td>
        将该组件
        <mark>
         置于水平方向的中央
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_centerVertical=“true”
       </td>
       <td>
        将该组件
        <mark>
         置于垂直方向的中央
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:layout_centerInParent=“true”
       </td>
       <td>
        将该组件
        <mark>
         置于水平方向和垂直方向的中央
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_RadioButton_158">
     </a>
     (八) 单选按钮【RadioButton】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰在布局中直接定义
      <code>
       RadioButton
      </code>
      组件，如果界面有多个
      <code>
       RadioButton
      </code>
      则表示可以多个，或全部选中；
      <br/>
      🔰与
      <code>
       RadioGroup
      </code>
      配合使用，这种方式定义下的
      <code>
       RadioButton
      </code>
      只可以选中一个；
      <br/>
      🔰一般
      <code>
       RadioButton
      </code>
      组件必须放在
      <code>
       RadioGroup
      </code>
      中才能达到效果；
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/ad11aeabb36a26144c3b8d26715c7aaf.png">
       <br/>
       🔰
       <strong>
        Radio Group的常用属性和方法
       </strong>
      </img>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名/方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:orientation=“horizontal”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置里面的RadioButton摆布方式
         </mark>
         ；
         <br/>
         horizontal(水平)
         <br/>
         vertical(垂直)
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         void clearCheck()
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          清除单选按钮中所有单选按钮的选中状态
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         int getCheckedRadioButtonId()
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          返回该单选按钮组中所选按钮的标识id
         </mark>
         ，如果没有勾选则返回-1
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         void setOnCheckedChangeListener()
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          注册一个当该按钮组中的单选按钮勾选状态发生改变时所要用的回调函数
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__171">
     </a>
     1. 单选按钮监听事件
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 三选一，点击那个，就那个显示在标签上</span>

    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_CheckBox_196">
     </a>
     (九) 复选框组件【CheckBox]
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       用于实现多个选项同时被选中的功能
      </strong>
      ，是Button的子类支持Button的所有属性
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/c06a18e3aae8e99edcc1f2d172b21aca.png">
       <br/>
       🔰多选按钮一般都是通过按钮的监听事件来监听。
      </img>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Spinner_201">
     </a>
     (十) 下拉列表框【Spinner】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       是ViewGroup的间接子类，因此可以作为容器使用；
      </strong>
      <br/>
      🔰在value下的strings.xml文件中添加数组作为数据来源；
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/2e9411bf0b4f41d4c03bc78f6f5cc772.png"/>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性/方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:spinnerMode
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          列表框的模式
         </mark>
         <br/>
         dialog：对话框风格的窗口
         <br/>
         dropdown：下拉菜单风格的窗口
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:entries=“@array/shuzu”
        </td>
        <td>
         使用数组资源
         <mark>
          设置改下拉列表的列表项目
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:dropDownWidth=“200px”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置下拉列表框的宽度
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:dropDownVerticalOffset=“60px”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置列表框的水平垂直距离
         <br/>
         <mark>
          下拉列表框整体往下移*单位
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:prompt=“@string/biaoti”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置
         <mark>
          对话框模式列表框的标题
         </mark>
         ，只能引用string.xml中的资源id，不能直接写字符串
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:dropDownSelector=“#F3A0A0”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          列表框被选中时的背景
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:popupBackground=“#F3A0A0”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置列表框的背景
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:dropDownHorizontalOffset
        </td>
        <td>
         设置列表框的水平偏移距离
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         void setSelection(int n)
        </td>
        <td>
         默认下拉列表框的第一项为选中项目，用这个方法指定第n个条目为选中条目
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         Object getSelectedItem()
        </td>
        <td>
         返回列表框中选中项
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__218">
     </a>
     1. 下拉列表步骤及事件监听
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰下拉列表的使用一般按如下步骤进行：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       在布局文件中定义控件
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>Spinner</span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>wrap_content<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@+id/dd<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="2">
      <li>
       在Activity中引用
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">Spinner</span> spinner <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Spinner</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dd<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> 
</code></pre>
     <ol start="3">
      <li>
       创建一个适配器(Array Adapter)为Spinner提供数据，Array Adapter中的数据来源于字符串数组和XML两种方式；
       <br/>
       方法一：使用字符串数组作为数据来源
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> provinces <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">"江苏省"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"浙江省"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"上海市"</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 设置Array Adapter</span>
<span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span> <span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> weekArray <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name"><span class="token namespace">android<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span>R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>simple_dropdown_item_1line<span class="token punctuation">,</span>provinces<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 三个参数分别为Context，布局文件，数组</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      方法二：使用XML作为数据来源，内容放到values目录下的strings.xml资源文件中
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>resources</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>string-array</span> <span class="token attr-name">name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>provinces_array<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>item</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>江苏省<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>item</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>item</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>浙江省<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>item</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>item</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>上海省<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>item</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>string-array</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>resources</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      设置Array Adapter
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span> provinceArray <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">createFromResource</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>array<span class="token punctuation">.</span>provinces_array<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name"><span class="token namespace">android<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span>R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>simple_spinner_item<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>    
provinceArray<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setDropDownViewResource</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name"><span class="token namespace">android<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span>R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>simple_spinner_dropdown_item<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="4">
      <li>
       将适配器与Spinner相关联
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">spinner<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>provinceArray<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="5">
      <li>
       创建一个监听器
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">SpinnerListener</span> <span class="token keyword">implements</span> <span class="token class-name">AdapterView<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnItemSelectedListener</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
       <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
       <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onItemSelected</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">AdapterView</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>arg0<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> arg1<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> arg2<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token keyword">long</span> arg3<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
           <span class="token class-name">String</span> selected <span class="token operator">=</span> arg0<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getItemAtPosition</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>arg2<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
           <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">makeText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"你所在的省份是："</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> selected<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_LONG<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
   <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="6">
      <li>
       绑定监听器
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">spinner<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnItemSelectedListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">SpinnerListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰如果开发者使用Spinner时己经可以确定列表选择框里的列表项，则完全不需要编写代码，也不需要设置适配器，直接使用android:entries属性来设置数组资源作为下拉列表框的列表项目，即可以省略(3)和(4)步骤。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_RatingBar_273">
     </a>
     (十一) 评分条【RatingBar】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       用星型来表示评分等级，设置时默认可以选择三种不同的风格；
      </strong>
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/2d8d338522e3d25beede0f9f0d3cd6ad.png"/>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:isIndicator=“false”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置是否可以与用户交互
         </mark>
         (默认true表示不可交互)
         <br/>
         设置用户是否可以点击
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:rating=“1.5”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          默认的评分数
         </mark>
         ，一开始就有的评分数
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:stepSize=“1.0”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          点击一次增长的长度
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:numStars=“5”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          表示星星数量
         </mark>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         style=“?android:ratingBarStyleIndicator”
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          设置风格
         </mark>
         <br/>
         <code>
          ?android:ratingBarStyle
         </code>
         大号星星
         <br/>
         <code>
          ?android:ratingBarStyleIndicator
         </code>
         正常星星
         <br/>
         <code>
          ?android:ratingBarStyleSmall
         </code>
         小号星星
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         float getRating(）
        </td>
        <td>
         <mark>
          获取当前评分
         </mark>
         ，与参数rating一致
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__284">
     </a>
     1. 星级进度改变时监听事件
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token comment">// 用RatingBar.OnRatingBarChangeListener()实现星级进度改变时触发事件</span>
<span class="token class-name">RatingBar</span> pingfen <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>pingfen<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">TextView</span> buchang <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>bu<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
pingfen<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnRatingBarChangeListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">RatingBar<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnRatingBarChangeListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
	<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onRatingChanged</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">RatingBar</span> ratingBar<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">float</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">boolean</span> b<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
		buchang<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"你的评分结果为:"</span><span class="token operator">+</span>pingfen<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getRating</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">""</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_FrameLayout_296">
     </a>
     (十二) 帧布局【FrameLayout】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       它是一种在Android终端屏幕上开辟一块空白区域的布局方式，放置在空白区域的组件必须对其到屏幕的左上角；
      </strong>
      <br/>
      🔰
      <strong>
       帧布局的大小由子元素中尺寸最大的那个来决定；
      </strong>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1TabHost_299">
     </a>
     1.【TabHost】组件
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       继承自FrameLayout，是带Tab选项卡的容器，包含
       <code>
        TabWidget
       </code>
       和
       <code>
        FrameLayout
       </code>
       两部分；
      </strong>
      <br/>
      🔰
      <code>
       TabWidget
      </code>
      是每个Tab选项卡标签按钮；
      <code>
       FrameLayout
      </code>
      是每个Tab选项卡的内容；
      <br/>
      <br/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2__303">
     </a>
     2. 定义布局文件
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Tab选项卡的用户界面布局文件的设计需要遵循下表的要求定义；
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         TabHost
        </td>
        <td>
         可自定义id
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         TabWidget
        </td>
        <td>
         必须设置
         <code>
          android:id
         </code>
         为
         <code>
          @android:id/tabs
         </code>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         FrameLayout
        </td>
        <td>
         必须设置为
         <code>
          android:id
         </code>
         为
         <code>
          @android:id/tabcontent
         </code>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="3__310">
     </a>
     3. 选项卡标签位置放置
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      <strong>
       1）放置用户界面顶部
      </strong>
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/222e2b8c913d76ce61ea4c7aa558f19d.png"/>
      <br/>
      <mark>
       布局内容需要用【LinearLayout来布局】；
      </mark>
      <br/>
      <br/>
      <strong>
       2）放置用户界面底部
      </strong>
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/7085940f852e285a3c663c4d189c8706.png"/>
      <br/>
      <mark>
       布局内容需要用【RelativeLayout】来布局，并且在【TabWidget】内添加
       <code>
        android:layout_alignParentBottom="true"
       </code>
      </mark>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="4_TabSpec_317">
     </a>
     4. TabSpec常用方法
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        方法名
       </th>
       <th>
        说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        setIndicator(CharSequence label
       </td>
       <td>
        用于
        <mark>
         指定选项卡显示的标签名
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        setIndicator(CharSequence label, Drawable icon)
       </td>
       <td>
        用于
        <mark>
         指定选项卡显示的标签名及图片
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        setIndicator(View view)
       </td>
       <td>
        用于
        <mark>
         指定选项卡显示的标签View
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        setContent(int viewId)
       </td>
       <td>
        用于
        <mark>
         指定选项卡显示的内容
        </mark>
        ，通常在布局文件中定义
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        setContent(Intent intent)
       </td>
       <td>
        用于
        <mark>
         指定选项卡显示的内容
        </mark>
        ，通常Inter用来封装启动另一个Activity
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        setCurrentTab(int index)
       </td>
       <td>
        <mark>
         用于指定默认选项卡
        </mark>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <h4>

                <span class="token comment">&lt;!--            简答题布局--&gt;</span>
            <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>LinearLayout</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
        <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>FrameLayout</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>LinearLayout</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>TabHost</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     🔰Java代码
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">TabHost</span> tabHost <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">TabHost</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>kaoshiXT<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 获取TabHost对象</span>
tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setup</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 通过setup()方法加载启动Tab Host</span>
tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTab</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">newTabSpec</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"tab01"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setIndicator</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"单选题"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setContent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>danxuan<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTab</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">newTabSpec</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"tab01"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setIndicator</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"多选题"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setContent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>duoxuan1<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addTab</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">newTabSpec</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"tab01"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setIndicator</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"简答题"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setContent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>jianda<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
tabHost<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setCurrentTab</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 指定2号选项卡为默认选项卡(选项卡自动0，1，2排序)</span>
</code></pre>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/3fb4772b1fd13bba5d66794554d6b2b0.png"/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_TableLayout_391">
     </a>
     (十三) 表格布局【TableLayout】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰该布局是由一系列行和列组成的网格，在这些网格的单元格中可以显示View组件；
      <br/>
      🔰它是和TableRow配合使用的一种常用的布局管理方式，
      <mark>
       每个TableRow对应表格里的一行
      </mark>
      ，
      <mark>
       TableRow的内容由单元格中的View组件组成
      </mark>
      ；
      <br/>
      🔰有多少个TableRow 就有多少行；
      <br/>
      🔰
      <strong>
       全局属性(列属性，写在TableLayout里面)
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:stretchColumns="* "
        </td>
        <td>
         设置允许被拉伸的列的序号
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:shrinkColumns="* "
        </td>
        <td>
         设置允许收缩的列的序号
         <br/>
         可以设置多个列，但必须用逗号隔开
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:collapseColumns=“1, 2”
        </td>
        <td>
         设置要隐藏的列的序号
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       单元格属性(单元格内书写)
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_column=“1”
        </td>
        <td>
         指定该单元格在第几列显示
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:layout_span=“2”
        </td>
        <td>
         合并2个单元格，即该组件占据2个单元格
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰在使用TableLayout布局设计APP界面布局时，需要注意以下几点：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       如果直接在TabLayout中添加组件(只添加一个)，那么该组件占满一行；
      </li>
      <li>
       如果一行上要放置多个组件，就必须添加TabRow容器，并将组件放置在TabRow容器中；
      </li>
      <li>
       TableRow中组件个数决定了该行有多少列，列的宽度由该列中最宽的单元格决定；
      </li>
      <li>
       TableRow的layout_width属性默认是match_parent; layout_height属性默认是wrap_content;
      </li>
      <li>
       整个表格布局的宽度取决于父容器的宽度；
      </li>
      <li>
       整个表格的行数由TableRow的数目及单独组件数目决定，列数由TableRow中最多个组件数决定；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰如果需要增加间隔线，可以在两个组件之间添加View，并设置该View的layout_height和background属性；
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>View</span>
	<span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">'</span>2dp<span class="token punctuation">'</span></span>
	<span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>background</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">'</span>#f00f00<span class="token punctuation">'</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <p>
     🔰实例
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token comment">&lt;!--表格布局--&gt;</span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>TableLayout</span> 
    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>shrinkColumns</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>*<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>stretchColumns</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>*<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token comment">&lt;!--    第一列--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>TableRow</span>
        <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
        <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
        <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>gravity</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>center_horizontal<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
        <span class="token comment">&lt;!--        单元格1 ，2， 3， 4， 5--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>TableRow</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    <span class="token comment">&lt;!--    第二列--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>TableRow</span>
        <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
        <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
        <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>gravity</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>center_horizontal<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
        <span class="token comment">&lt;!--        单元格1 ，2， 3， 4， 5--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>TableRow</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
    <span class="token comment">&lt;!--    第三列--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>TableRow</span>
	    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
	    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
	    <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>gravity</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>center_horizontal<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
        <span class="token comment">&lt;!--        单元格1 ，2， 3， 4， 5--&gt;</span>
    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>TableRow</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>TableLayout</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="__456">
     </a>
     四. 高级界面组件与布局
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Adapter_457">
     </a>
     (一) Adapter适配器基础
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Adapter是一个接口。在进行高级界面设计时，需要使用Adapter将数据源绑定到指定的View上。常见的ListView，GridView等都需要用到Adapter。
      <br/>
      🔰常用子类有ListAdapter，BaseAdapter，ArrayAdapter，SimpleAdapter，SimpleCursorAdapter等。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_ListAdapter_460">
     </a>
     1. ListAdapter
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰ListAdapter是一个直接继承于Adapter的接口类，
      <mark>
       它是ListView和数据之间的接口
      </mark>
      ，通常数据来源于一个Cursor(游标)，用于显示ListAdapter中的数据；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_BaseAdapter_462">
     </a>
     2. BaseAdapter
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <mark>
       BaseAdapter是ListAdapter和SpinnerAdapter接口的抽象类
      </mark>
      ，通过重写View getView(int position, View convertView, ViewGroup parent)，int getCount()，long getItemId(int position)和Object getItem(int position)四个方法，可以实现复杂的用户界面布局；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="3_ArrayAdapter_464">
     </a>
     3. ArrayAdapter
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰ArrayAdapter是继承与BaseAdapter的一个具体类。默认情况下，
      <mark>
       ArrayAdapter绑定每个对象的字符串值到系统默认布局的TextVIew或开发者自定义的TextView上，每行只能显示一个文本
      </mark>
      ；
      <br/>
      🔰常用的构造方法：
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Context</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> resource<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">T</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> object<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol>
      <li>
       第一个参数为上下文；
      </li>
      <li>
       第二个参数包含一个TextView， 用来填充ListView的每一行布局资源；
      </li>
      <li>
       第三个参数为ListView上每一行具体要显示的数据；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰实际运用：在List View部分有实际运用；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__Android__475">
     </a>
     1) Android 系统提供的布局资源及功能说明
    </h5>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th align="left">
        布局资源
       </th>
       <th align="left">
        功能
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td align="left">
        android.R.layout.simple_list_item_1
       </td>
       <td align="left">
        每一项只有一个TextView
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td align="left">
        android.R.layout.simple_list_item_multiple_choice
       </td>
       <td align="left">
        每一项有一个复选框，需要用setChoiceMode()方法设置选择模式(ListView.CHOICE_MODE_MULTIPLE【多选模式】)
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td align="left">
        android.R.layout.simple_list_item_checked
       </td>
       <td align="left">
        每一项有一个选择项，需要用setChoiceMode()方法设置选择模式(ListView.CHOICE_MODE_MULTIPLE【多选模式】)
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td align="left">
        android.R.layout.simple_list_item_single_choice
       </td>
       <td align="left">
        每一项有一个单选按钮，需要用setChoiceMode()方法设置选择模式(ListView.CHOICE_MODE_SINGLE 【单选模式】)
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <h4>
     <a id="4_SimpleAdapter_482">
     </a>
     4. SimpleAdapter
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰SimpleAdapter是继承与BaseAdapter的一个具体类。它可以根据开发者的要求
      <mark>
       在每一行上显示图片，文本等复杂的布局对象
      </mark>
      ，可以自定义出各种效果显示在ListView的每一行上；
      <br/>
      🔰构造方法：
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token class-name">SimpleAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Context</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">List</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token keyword">extends</span> <span class="token class-name">Map</span><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>data<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> resource<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> from<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token keyword">to</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol>
      <li>
       参数1为上下文；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数2为用HashMap(String, Object)构造的List；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数3为ListView上显示的每行布局文件的ID；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数4为HashMap中所有键构成的字符串数组；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数5为ListView上每一行布局文件中对应组件ID构成int型数组；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰运用顺序：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       在主布局文件上布局LIst View组件；
      </li>
      <li>
       新建一个布局文件item，布局一行显示的自定义效果；
      </li>
      <li>
       Java代码：
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ListView</span> lv <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lv<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">int</span> imgid<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>caocao<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>guanyu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>huangzhong<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>liubei<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> itemname<span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">"曹操"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"关羽"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"黄忠"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"刘备"</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 下面7行代码用于为 SimpleAdapter 准备 HashMap 构成的 List 数据集</span>
<span class="token class-name">ArrayList</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">HashMap</span><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Object</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>itemlist <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ArrayList</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token keyword">for</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">int</span> i<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> i<span class="token operator">&lt;</span>imgid<span class="token punctuation">.</span>length<span class="token punctuation">;</span> i<span class="token operator">++</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token comment">// HashMap 构成 List 数据集</span>
	<span class="token class-name">HashMap</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Object</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> map<span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">HashMap</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	map<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">put</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"itemimg"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> imgid<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	map<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">put</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"itemname"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> itemname<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	itemlist<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>map<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token comment">// 用于指定数据源与 ListView 的每一行中每个显示项对应的键</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> from <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">"itemimg"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"itemname"</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 用于指定 ListView 的每一行中每个显示项对应键的值填充到对应组件的ID</span>
<span class="token keyword">int</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token keyword">to</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>img<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// Simple Adapter 装配数据</span>
<span class="token class-name">SimpleAdapter</span> simpleAdapter<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">SimpleAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> itemlist<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>item<span class="token punctuation">,</span>from<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token keyword">to</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 将Adapter与ListVIew关联</span>
lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>simpleAdapter<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="5_SimpleCuisorAdapter_519">
     </a>
     5. SimpleCuisorAdapter
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <mark>
       SimpleCuisorAdapter用于绑定数据库中的数据
      </mark>
      ，它有以下的构造方法。
      <br/>
      ``
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ListView_523">
     </a>
     (二) 显示模板【ListView】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰以列表方式显示内容，必须包含三个关键元素：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       ListView 中每一行的View；
      </li>
      <li>
       填入View中的数据可以是被映射的字符串，图片或基本组件；
      </li>
      <li>
       连接数据与ListView的Adapter；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ListView</span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>wrap_content<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@+id/lv<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span> <span class="token keyword">extends</span> <span class="token class-name">AppCompatActivity</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
   <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span> adapter<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
   <span class="token keyword">private</span> <span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span> item <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span><span class="token string">"周一"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"周二"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"周三"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"周四"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"周五"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"周六"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"周天"</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

       <span class="token class-name">ListView</span> lv <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lv<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token comment">// 为ArrayAdapter装配数据</span>
       adapter <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ArrayAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name"><span class="token namespace">android<span class="token punctuation">.</span></span>R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>simple_list_item_single_choice<span class="token punctuation">,</span> item<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> 
       <span class="token comment">// 将Adapter与ListVIew关联</span>
       lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setAdapter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>adapter<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token comment">// 设置选择模式(单选模式)</span>
       lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setChoiceMode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">ListView</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>CHOICE_MODE_SINGLE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token comment">// 设置单击监听事件(单选项)</span>
       lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnItemClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">AdapterView<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnItemClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
           <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
           <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onItemClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">AdapterView</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> adapterView<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> view<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">long</span> l<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                <span class="token comment">// 单击某项，转为Text View类型</span>
               <span class="token class-name">TextView</span> tv <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">TextView</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>view<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">makeText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> tv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">":"</span><span class="token operator">+</span>item<span class="token punctuation">[</span>i<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_SHORT<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token comment">// tv.getText().toString()：获取Text View上的文本信息</span>

           <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
       <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">-</span>
       <span class="token comment">// 设置选择模式(多选模式)</span>
       lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setChoiceMode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">ListView</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>CHOICE_MODE_MULTIPLE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

       lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnItemClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">AdapterView<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnItemClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
