                   <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>checked<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">get</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>j<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token comment">// 如果该位置被选中</span>
                       str<span class="token operator">+=</span>item<span class="token punctuation">[</span>j<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

               <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
               <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">makeText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> str<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_SHORT<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_ListView__582">
     </a>
     1. ListView 设置监听事件
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰单击，调用setOnItemClickListener()方法；
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ListView</span> lv <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lv<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnItemClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">AdapterView<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnItemClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
	<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onItemClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">AdapterView</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> adapterView<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> view<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">long</span> l<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>                
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰长按，调用setOnItemLongClickListener()方法；
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ListView</span> lv <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>lv<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
lv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnItemLongClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token operator">&gt;</span><span class="token class-name">AdapterView<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnItemLongClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	 <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
	<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">boolean</span> <span class="token function">onItemLongClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">AdapterView</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> adapterView<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> view<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> i<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">long</span> l<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
		<span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol>
      <li>
       参数1表示事件发生的AdapterView；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数2表示单击或长按的ListView的某一项View；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数3表示单击或长按的这一项在Adapter中的位置；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数4表示单击或长按的这一项在ListView中的位置；
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Intent_607">
     </a>
     (三) Intent触发器
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰在Android系统的四个核心组件中，除了Contentprovider以
      <br/>
      外，其他三个核心组件（Activity、Service、Broadcast
      <br/>
      receiver）实际上都是被一个叫做
      <mark>
       Intent的异步消息来激活的
      </mark>
      。
      <br/>
      🔰激活的组件可以是Android系统自身提供的，也以是开发者
      <br/>
      自定义的，其激活方式有
      <mark>
       显式Intent
      </mark>
      和
      <mark>
       隐式Intent
      </mark>
      两种。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰一个Intent对象可以包含以下六个信息：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       ComponentName(组件名称)：指明Intent对象的组件名称，是一个可选项，如果被设置，Intent对象就显式指定了要转向的组件。
      </li>
      <li>
       Action(动作)：指明Intent要完成的一个动作，是在Intent-Filter中指定字符串常量；该字符可以在App的配置文件中定义，也可以是系统自带的。Intent不用直接指明这个组件。交给Android去根据IntentFilter做匹配筛选，选择符合的组件去启动
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      <strong>
       Action常用常量和功能说明
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         常量值
        </th>
        <th align="left">
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.action.MAIN
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         应用程序入口
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.action.VIEW
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         显示数据给用户
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.action.DIAL
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         电话拨号并显示拨号用户界面
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.action.CALL
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         直接打电话
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.action.SEND
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         直接发送短信
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.action.SENDTO
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         选择对象发短信
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <ol start="3">
      <li>
       Data(数据)：通常用于向系统提供数据，即Action需要的数据，一般用URL和对应的MIME类型来表示，也是在IntentFIlter 中定义的。例如，如果动作是ACTION_VIEW，则需要提供访问目标URI(用http://URI表示)数据。
      </li>
      <li>
       Category(类别)：用于为Action提供额外的附加类别信息，也是IntentFilter中的字符串常量；一个Intent对象只能设置一个Action，但是可以设置多个Category。Category和Action通常在IntentFilter中使用，用于实现隐式Intent。Category可以直接使用系统定义的，也可以由开发者自己定义。
      </li>
     </ol>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         常量值
        </th>
        <th align="left">
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.category.LAUNCHER
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         程序最优先启动的Activity
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         android.intent.category.HOME
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         程序启动后显示的第一个界面
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <ol start="5">
      <li>
       Extras(扩展域)：用于Intent对象附加一个或多个键值对信息，该键值对是一个Bundle对象。
      </li>
      <li>
       Flags(标志)：用于告诉Android如何启动Activity，启动后如何处理。
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰可用IntentFilter过滤不满足条件的组件。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_IntentFilter_638">
     </a>
     1. IntentFilter
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰IntentFilter负责过滤所提供的组件功能。
      <br/>
      🔰IntentFilter是由动作(Activity)，类别(Category)和数据(Data)构成的一种过滤筛选机制。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_Intent_641">
     </a>
     2. 显式Intent
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰显式Intent：
      <mark>
       通过指定目标组件名称来启动组件，并且每次启动的组件只能有一个。
      </mark>
      <br/>
      🔰一般情况下由于开发者不知道其他应用程序的组件名称，所以
      <mark>
       显式Intent通常用于启动应用程序内部组件；
      </mark>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰在Activity中通过调用startActivity()或startActivityForResult()方法，在方法参数中传递Intent对象，实现不同Activity间的切换和数据传递。
      <br/>
      🔰显示Intent启动Activity：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       实现直接指定需要打开的Activity对应类。
       <br/>
       例如：单击Button可以实现从A_Activity跳转到B_Activity，需创建两个对应的Java文件和对应的布局文件；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">tvAdd<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>tvadd<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
tvAdd<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">View<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token comment">// 显示Intent启动Activity</span>
	<span class="token comment">// MainActivity.this  目前的文件   AddActivity.class  需要打开的文件，以class结尾</span>
	<span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Intent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">AddActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">startActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intent<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="3_Intent_662">
     </a>
     3. 隐式Intent
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰隐式Intent：
      <mark>
       不指定要启动的目标组件名称，而是指定Intent的Action、Data或Category等；
       <br/>
       🔰通常用隐式Intent激活其他应用程序中的组件；
      </mark>
      <br/>
      🔰在启动组件时，会去匹配AndroidManifest.xml 相关组件的Intent-filter，并逐一匹配出满足属性的组件，当不止一个满足时就会弹出一个让用户选择启动哪个目标组件的对话框。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰隐式Intent启动Activity：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       隐式启动是指Android根据过滤规则自动匹配对应的Intent，不需要明确指明。可以启动App自身的Activity，也可以是内置的，或者第三方App提供。
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰在AndroidMainfest.xml中添加AddActivity中的intent filter属性，将categroy的属性设为
      <code>
       android.intent.category.DEFAULT
      </code>
      。
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>activity</span>
	<span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>.add_layout<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
	<span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>exported</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>false<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
	<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>intent-filter</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
		<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>action</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>app.java.MYACTION<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
		<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>category</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>android.intent.category.DEFAULT<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
	<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>intent-filter</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>activity</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰在MainActivity.java中点击文本监听事件设置Intent发送的Action为
      <code>
       app.java.MYACTION
      </code>
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">add<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">View<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
	<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> view<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
		<span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Intent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
		<span class="token comment">// Action 的 name 与 xml 中的匹配</span>
		intent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setAction</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"app.java.MYACTION"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
		<span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">startActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intent<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰如果Activity支持接收隐式Intent，就一定要在intent filter中加入category属性值"android.intent.category.DEFAULT“。
      <br/>
      🔰如果开发的APP要明确拒绝被别的APP启动某一个Activity，就需要在配置清单文件的Activity标签中设置exported的属性值为false。
      <br/>
      <strong>
       Intent调用其他常用组件
      </strong>
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/58ef8ce73a2d6d6417db5272d539a9a6.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="4__700">

    <h4>
     <a id="6_Intent_732">
     </a>
     6. Intent传递数据
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰当
      <mark>
       一次传递一个数据
      </mark>
      时，可以直接调用Intent的putExtra()方法存入数据；在获得Intent后调用getXXXExtra()方法获得对应的数据。
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">A_Activity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>java 文件

add<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">View<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
           <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
           <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> view<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
               <span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Intent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> add_layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> s <span class="token operator">=</span> add<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token comment">// 存入数据</span>
               intent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putExtra</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"edts"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token function">startActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intent<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
           <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
       <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">-</span>
<span class="token class-name">B_Activity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>java 文件

<span class="token comment">// 获取对应的数据</span>
<span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIntent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 传入字符串，名字与上方要一样</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> s <span class="token operator">=</span> intent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getStringExtra</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"edts"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
text<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>s<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰当
      <mark>
       一次传递多个数据
      </mark>
      时，可以使用Bundle对象作为容器，通过调用Bundle的putXXX()方法先将数据存储到Bundle中，接着调用Intent的putExtras()方法将Bundle存入Intent中，然后在获得Intent以后调用getExtras()获得Bundle容器，最后调用其getXXX()方法获取对应的数据。
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">A_Activity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>java 文件

add<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">View<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
           <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
           <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> view<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
               <span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Intent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> add_layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">Bundle</span> bundle <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Bundle</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> zh <span class="token operator">=</span> zhanghao<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> mm <span class="token operator">=</span> mima<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token comment">// 利用Bundle存储多个数据</span>
               bundle<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"zhanghao"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> zh<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               bundle<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"mima"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> mm<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token comment">// 存入Intent</span>
               intent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putExtras</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>bundle<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token function">startActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intent<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
           <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
       <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">--</span><span class="token operator">-</span>
<span class="token class-name">B_Activity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>java 文件

<span class="token comment">// 获取对应的数据</span>
<span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getIntent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 获得Bundle容器</span>
<span class="token class-name">Bundle</span> bundle <span class="token operator">=</span> intent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getExtras</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// 获取对应数据</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> zhangh <span class="token operator">=</span> bundle<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"zhanghao"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">String</span> mim <span class="token operator">=</span> bundle<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"mima"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Fragment_789">
     </a>
     (四) 碎片化组件【Fragment】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Fragment碎片化组件，用于提高代码重用性，改善用户体验和适应大屏幕的需求；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/28805da0b16d44c2f3aaa32771ec66ad.png"/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/2f53f4a81eda779f788ed0fbc1fc1708.png"/>
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/0a31c1d662d8d3eafb68c1abf4a0c96e.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_Fragment__795">
     </a>
     1. Fragment 布局文件的创建
    </h4>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/8b991cbb8b375fd90dd2aafaba50a9f7.png"/>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/c925e210b0a772ddb5cba5fd22b2a86e.png"/>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/add059c32706f2092589687263a9d594.png"/>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/7bd6f8078eaf4c0aee049c1d75e319e2.png"/>
    </p>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/28e9defc8e7cbf4054cfe2de3235cde3.png"/>
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       参数1是需要加载的布局文件名；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数2为返回的VIew对象；
      </li>
      <li>
       参数3为true表示表示将root作为根对象返回，否则为false表示将这个root对象的布局参数属性附加到根布局对象上。
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ViewViewPager_804">
     </a>
     (五) View的左右滑屏切换【ViewPager】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <mark>
       ViewPager手势滑动完成View的左右滑屏切换
      </mark>
      ，可以作为引导页，图片轮播等功能。
      <br/>
      🔰继承了ViewGroup类，也是一个容器类，可在其中添加其他的View类。
      <br/>
      🔰相关实例内容请看
      <a href="https://blog.csdn.net/qq_51712954/article/details/126549524?csdn_share_tail=%7B%22type%22:%22blog%22,%22rType%22:%22article%22,%22rId%22:%22126549524%22,%22source%22:%22qq_51712954%22%7D">
       【Android——APP引导页，图片轮播功能实现】
      </a>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_PagerTitleStrip_809">
     </a>
     1. PagerTitleStrip
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰是ViewPage的一个关于当前页，上一页，下一页非交互性指示器，相当于每个页面的标题。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_PagerTabStrip_812">
     </a>
     2. PagerTabStrip
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰PagerTabStrip是ViewPage的一个关于当前页，上一页，下一页交互性指示器，会由一条下划线提示当前在那一页，且单击Tab时，会跳转到该页面。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ViewFlipper_816">
     </a>
     (六) 左右轮播及上下轮播【ViewFlipper】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰ViewFlipper 一般用于图片的切换，当然也可以添加用户自定义的View 或其他 View 对象，并实现View的切换。
      <br/>
      🔰
      <strong>
       ViewAnimator 相关方法及功能说明
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         方法
        </th>
        <th align="left">
         功能
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setInAnimation
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         设置View进入屏幕时使用的动画，可以直接传入Animation对象，也可以传入定义的Animation文件的
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setOutAnimation
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         设置VIew退出屏幕时使用的动画，使用方法和setInAnimation方法一样
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         showNext
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         显示FrameLayout里面的下一个View
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         showPrevious
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         显示Framelayout里面的上一个View
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       ViewFilpper 相关方法及功能说明
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         方法
        </th>
        <th align="left">
         功能
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setFlipInterval
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         设置View切换的时间间隔。单位：毫秒
         <br/>
         2000毫秒 ==2秒
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         startFlipping
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         开始进行View的切换，切换会循环进行
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         stopFlipping
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         停止View切换
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setAutoStart
        </td>
        <td align="left">
         设置是否自动开始，如果为true，则当ViewFlipper显示的时候View的切换会自动开始
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰自动轮播也可以根据用户需求，通过手势来实现图片的轮播效果。即当用户向左滑屏时，图片向左滚动切换。实例：
      <a href="https://blog.csdn.net/qq_51712954/article/details/126567387?csdn_share_tail=%7B%22type%22:%22blog%22,%22rType%22:%22article%22,%22rId%22:%22126567387%22,%22source%22:%22qq_51712954%22%7D">
       【手势实现左右滑屏切换】
      </a>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__835">
     </a>
     1. 左右轮播图
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_836">
     </a>
     1）已知图片资源个数
    </h5>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰布局代码
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ViewFlipper</span>

       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ImageView</span>

    <h5>
     <a id="2_859">

     2）图片资源个数未知

     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ViewFlipper</span>

    <h4>
     <a id="2__882">
     </a>
     2. 上下轮播
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰res文件夹右键，新 建 Directory 文件 夹 ， 取名为anim；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/89b0b754a7b35ae390f8fb2b8643ce21.png"/>
      <br/>
      🔰anim文件夹右键，新建两个Animation文 件 ， 分别取名为anim_comein.xml, anim_getout.xml；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/422436fc9705c332d2e510eca5f60565.png"/>
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml">anim_comein.xml

<span class="token prolog">&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;</span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>set</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">xmlns:</span>android</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>translate</span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>fromXDelta</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>100%p<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>toXDelta</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>0<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>duration</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>1000<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>set</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
______________________________________
anim_getout.xml

<span class="token prolog">&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;</span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>set</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">xmlns:</span>android</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>translate</span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>fromYDelta</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>0<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>toYDelta</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>-100%p<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>duration</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>1000<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>set</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      <code>
       android:toXDelta="100%"
      </code>
      : 表示自身的100%，也就是从View自己的位置开始；
      <br/>
      <code>
       android:toXDelta="80%p"
      </code>
      : 表示父层View的80%，是以它父层View为参照的。
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/e1851adb3917fa9a55102aa877633cd0.png"/>
     </p>
     <p>
      🔰布局代码
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ViewFlipper</span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@+id/flipper<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
       <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>inAnimation</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@anim/anim_comein<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>	 <span class="token attr-name">&lt;!--进入时动画效果--</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
       android:outAnimation="@anim/anim_getout"   <span class="token comment">&lt;!--离开时动画效果--&gt;</span>
       android:flipInterval="2000"&gt;   <span class="token comment">&lt;!--切换时长2s--&gt;</span>

       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>ImageView</span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_width</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>layout_height</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>match_parent<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>scaleType</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>fitXY<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>src</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@mipmap/retouch_20210209121016<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
           ……该部分设置需要需要轮播的图片资源
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>ViewFlipper</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰功能代码(在 onCreate()方法中设置 )
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ViewFlipper</span> viewFlipper <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>flipper<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
viewFlipper<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">startFlipping</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">// 实现轮播效果</span>
</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_RecyclerView_937">
     </a>
     (七) 【RecyclerView】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰RecyclerView 是 Android 5.0 开始推出的用来替代 ListView 和 GrindView 的组件；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_RecyclerView_939">
     </a>
     1. 导入RecyclerView包
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      1、导入RecyclerView包：
      <code>
       build
      </code>
      —&gt;
      <code>
       Edit Libraries and Dependencies
      </code>
      ;
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/24b2225f84407803cf380dd8958cac9b.png"/>
      <br/>
      2、选 中 app ， 点 击 DeclaredDependencies 中 的 + 号 ， 选 择Library Dependency;
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/0e82556584b128f162b9e2cde3b1570b.png"/>
      <br/>
      3、输入recycler查找相关包，选择第一个，点击OK等待系统自动下载并加载
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/a3e3ab23e13f04f4442aa28039985eb6.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_RecyclerViewLayoutManager_945">
     </a>
     2. RecyclerView.LayoutManager
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰RecyclerView.LayoutManager是一个抽象类，它包含下面的
      <br/>
      三个子类：
     </p>
     <blockquote>
      <p>
       1、LinearLayoutManager：线性布局管理器
       <br/>
       • LinearLayoutManager类有两种常用的构造方法。
      </p>
      <ol>
       <li>
        第一种构造方法格式如下：
       </li>
      </ol>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">LinearLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Context</span> context<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">//  context参数为上下文，实现的是默认的垂直布局</span>
mRecycleView<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">LinearLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
      <ol start="2">
       <li>
        第二种构造方法格式如下：
       </li>
      </ol>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">LinearLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span> <span class="token class-name">Context</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> orientation<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">boolean</span> reverseLayout<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">// 第一个参数context为上下文，第二个参数orientation为布局显示方式，第三个参数reverseLayout为是否反转。</span>
<span class="token class-name">LinearLayoutManager</span> linerLayoutManager <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">LinearLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">LinearLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>HORIZONTAL<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
mRecycleView<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>linerLayoutManager<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
      <p>
       <strong>
        orientation参数值及功能说明
       </strong>
      </p>
      <table>
       <thead>
        <tr>
         <th>
          参数值
         </th>
         <th>
          功能
         </th>
        </tr>
       </thead>
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <td>
          LinearLayoutManager.VERTICAL
         </td>
         <td>
          不反转的垂直布局：数据从上往下加载(新数据在底部)
          <br/>
          反转的垂直布局：数据从下向上加载(新数据在顶部)
         </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
         <td>
          LinearLayoutManager.HORIZONTAL
         </td>
         <td>
          不反转的水平布局：数据从左到右加载(新数据在右)
          <br/>
          反转的水平布局：数据从右向左加载(新数据在左)
         </td>
        </tr>
       </tbody>
      </table>
     </blockquote>
     <blockquote>
      <p>
       2、StaggeredGridLayoutManager: 错列网格布局管理器
       <br/>
       • 构 造方法格式如下：
      </p>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">StaggeredGridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intspanCount<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token keyword">int</span> orientation<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">// 第 一个参数 spanCount 为要显示的列数 ， 第二个参数orientation为显示的方向</span>
<span class="token class-name">StaggeredGridLayoutManager</span> staggeredGridLayoutManager <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">StaggeredGridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token class-name">StaggeredGridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>VERTICAL<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
mRecycleView<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>staggeredGridLayoutManager<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     </blockquote>
     <blockquote>
      <p>
       3、GridLayoutManager：网格布局管理器
       <br/>
       • 既可以设置列数，也可以设置方向，还可以设置加载数据是否反 转 ， 其功能可以理解 为 LinearLayoutManager 和StaggeredGridLayoutManager结合体。
       <br/>
       • 它有两种构造方法:
      </p>
      <ol>
       <li>
        第一种构造方法格式如下：
       </li>
      </ol>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">GridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Context</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> spanCount<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">// 第一个参数context为上下文，第二个参数spanCount为显示列数，默认显示方向为垂直布局</span>
</code></pre>
      <ol start="2">
       <li>
        第二种构造方法格式如下：
       </li>
      </ol>
      <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">GridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Context</span> context<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> spanCount<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">int</span> orientation<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">boolean</span> reverseLayout<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
<span class="token comment">// 第一个参数context为上下 文 ， 第二个 参 数 spanCount 为显示列数 ， </span>
<span class="token comment">// 第三个 参 数orientation为显示方向，第四个参数reverseLayout为是否反转。</span>
<span class="token class-name">GridLayoutManager</span> gridLayoutManager<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">GridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token class-name">GridLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>VERTICAL<span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
mRecycleView<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setLayoutManager</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>gridLayoutManager<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     </blockquote>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="__995">
     </a>
     五. 菜单和对话框
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="__996">
     </a>
     (一) 菜单
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__ContextMenu__997">
     </a>
     1. ContextMenu (上下文菜单)
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰ContextMenu (上下文菜单) ：在某个组件或视图上长按(超过2s)弹出；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/4d7f575a553d62e47ee4568131d64bbf.png"/>
      <br/>
      🔰菜单设置：
      <br/>
      1.1
      <strong>
       在Activity中添加onCreateContextMenu()方法:
      </strong>
      <br/>
      》白位置右键 – Generate – Override Methods – 输入contextmenu，选择onCreateContextMenu()
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/00f82011265a82ba79161931a9211090.png"/>
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
   <span class="token keyword">protected</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCreate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Bundle</span> savedInstanceState<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
       <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">onCreate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>savedInstanceState<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token function">setContentView</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>activity_main<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token class-name">EditText</span> editText <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rv<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token comment">// 为组件添加加ContextMenu</span>
       <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">registerForContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editText<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

   <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
   <span class="token comment">// 参数1加载的上下文菜单；  参数2与菜单相关的组件；   参数3菜单的附加信息；</span>
   <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCreateContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">ContextMenu</span> menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">ContextMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ContextMenuInfo</span> menuInfo<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
       <span class="token comment">// 填充菜单资源</span>
       <span class="token class-name">MenuInflater</span> inflater <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getMenuInflater</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token comment">// 参数1是待转换菜单xml；  参数2是菜单对象；</span>
       inflater<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">inflate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span>main_menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> menu<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

       <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">onCreateContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> menuInfo<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      2.1
      <strong>
       设置Xml文件菜单项
      </strong>
      <br/>
      1）res右键–Directory–menu–新建main_menu.xml文件
      <br/>
      2）menu右键–New–Menu Resource File， 新建一个名为main_menu.xml文件
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml">main_menu.xml
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>menu</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">xmlns:</span>android</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>group</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@+id/gbackcolor<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>item</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@+id/bgreen<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>title</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>背景绿色<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
       <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>item</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>id</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>@+id/bblue<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
           <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>title</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>背景蓝色<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
   <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>group</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>menu</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔹菜单的XML文件包含menu、group和item三个元素；
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       menu：定义一个菜单，可包含一个或多个
       <code>
        &lt;group&gt;
       </code>
       和
       <code>
        &lt;item&gt;
       </code>
       元素；
      </li>
      <li>
       group：对菜单进行分组，可以以组的形式操作菜单项，也可以省略
      </li>
     </ol>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:id
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单组的id
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:orderInCategory
        </td>
        <td>
         定义该组菜单在总菜单中的默认次序，整数值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:checkableBehavior
        </td>
        <td>
         定义该组菜单是否可选:none(默认值，不可选)\all(多选)\single(单选)
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:visible
        </td>
        <td>
         设置该组菜单是否可见，true或false
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:enabled
        </td>
        <td>
         设置该组菜单是否可用，true或false
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <ol start="3">
      <li>
       item：代表菜单中的一个选项。常用属性有id、icon和title等
      </li>
     </ol>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:id
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项的id
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:title
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项的标题
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:icon
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项的图标
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:alphabeticShortcut
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项的字母快捷键
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:numericShortcut
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项的数字快捷键
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:checkable
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项是否可选，true或false
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:checked
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项是否为选中状态，true或false
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:visible
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单项是否可见，true或false
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      2.2
      <strong>
       直接使用Java代码在onCreateContextMenu（）中添加
       <br/>
       菜单项
      </strong>
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCreateContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">ContextMenu</span> menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">ContextMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ContextMenuInfo</span> menuInfo<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
       menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"背景绿色"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"背景蓝色"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"前景蓝色"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">3</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"前景绿色"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">onCreateContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> menuInfo<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_1070">
     </a>
     1）上下文菜单一般运用方式
    </h5>
    <p>
     • 实现性别选择功能（ContextMenu上下文菜单）；
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
    <span class="token keyword">protected</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCreate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Bundle</span> savedInstanceState<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">onCreate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>savedInstanceState<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token function">setContentView</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span>activity_main<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        editText <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>rv<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">registerForContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>editText<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    
    <span class="token comment">// 创建上下文菜单</span>
    <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCreateContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">ContextMenu</span> menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">ContextMenu<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ContextMenuInfo</span> menuInfo<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">onCreateContextMenu</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>menu<span class="token punctuation">,</span> v<span class="token punctuation">,</span> menuInfo<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setHeaderTitle</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"性别"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"男"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        menu<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">add</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"女"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token comment">// 单击上下文菜单后的实现</span>
    <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
    <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">boolean</span> <span class="token function">onContextItemSelected</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MenuItem</span> item<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token keyword">switch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getItemId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">case</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token operator">:</span>
                editText<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"男"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token keyword">break</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            <span class="token keyword">case</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token operator">:</span>
                editText<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"女"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token keyword">break</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
        <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">onContextItemSelected</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>item<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="2__OptionsMenu__1100">
     </a>
     2. OptionsMenu (选项菜单)
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰 OptionsMenu (选项菜单) ：最常见的菜单，分为Icon按钮、Item按钮和overflow按钮；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/c7801de0ddf88071b2844d45884eafe1.png"/>
      <br/>
      🔰
      <code>
       public boolean onCreateOptionsMenu(Menu menu);
      </code>
      在该方法中完成菜单初始化；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/edc5f096321f7c6a376bdeb60debca7c.png"/>
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <code>
       public boolean onOptionsItemSelected(@NonNull MenuItem item);
      </code>
      菜单选项被选中时触发，在该方法中完成事件处理。
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/87522f35f87d9a2fcf5163339e5bf707.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="3__SubMenu__1110">
     </a>
     3. SubMenu (子菜单)
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰 SubMenu (子菜单)：将功能相同和相似的分组进行多级显示，但子菜单不能再嵌套子菜单；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/e739984b917925ef7d8e02558f21a807.png"/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/8e9fca4867973e18c3036987de645c48.png"/>
      <br/>
      <strong>
       SubMenu常用方法及功能说明
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         subMenu.setHeaderIcon(R.mipmap.ic_launcher_round);
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单头的图标
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         subMenu.setHeaderTitle(“选择居住的城市”);
        </td>
        <td>
         设置菜单头的标题
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         subMenu.setIcon(R.mipmap.ic_launcher);
        </td>
        <td>
         设置子菜单图标
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰
      <code>
       public boolean onCreateOptionsMenu(Menu menu);
      </code>
      SubMenu创建；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/d0fc2c344ac2b981d6cdc840793cff23.png"/>
      <br/>
      🔰
      <code>
       public boolean onOptionsItemSelected(@NonNull MenuItem item);
      </code>
      菜单选项被选中时触发，在该方法中完成事件处理。
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/87d0b45e29282982e601297b8fb83022.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="1ActionBar_1124">
     </a>

      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/c4af9e92785781545ad9d8b770a269a3.png"/>
