    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="4___PopupMenu_1143">
     </a>
     4. PopupMenu(弹出式菜单)
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰 PopupMenu(弹出式菜单) ：用于在指定的VIew下显示一个弹出菜单，其菜单选项通常由XML菜单资源文件生成。
      <br/>
      <strong>
       PopupMenu的相关方法及功能说明
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         PopupMenu(Context context, View anchor)
        </td>
        <td>
         第一个参数表示Activity，第二个参数表示弹出菜单显示在指定anchor控件的下方或上方
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         MenuInflater.inflate(int menuResId, PopupMenu.getMenu())
        </td>
        <td>
         加载XML菜单资源到弹出菜单对象中
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setOnMenuItemClickListener()
        </td>
        <td>
         设置弹出菜单项的单击事件
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         show()
        </td>
        <td>
         弹出菜单
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         dismiss()
        </td>
        <td>
         关闭菜单
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰使用步骤：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       在res/menu文件创建XML菜单资源文件；
      </li>
      <li>
       在Activity中绑定Text View的单击监听事件；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/3c28afdacef7f6fdc32a7bf43d07ee59.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1165">
     </a>
     (二) 对话框
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰 Android提供普通(含提示消息和按钮)、列表、单选、多选、等待、进度条、编辑和自定义等多种形式的对话框。
      <br/>
      🔰 Dialog 直接子类有 AlertDialog( 提示对话框 ) 和CharacterPickerDialog(字符选择对话框);
      <br/>
      🔰 间接子类有DatePickerDialog (日期选择对话框) 、TimePickerDialog ( 时间选择对话框 ) 和ProgressDialog (进度对话框)等；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_AlertDialog___1170">
     </a>
     1. AlertDialog( 提示对话框 )
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰AlertDialog提示对话框可以生成四种预定义的对话框：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       带消息和按钮的提示对话框；
      </li>
      <li>
       带列表和按钮的列表对话框；
      </li>
      <li>
       带单选列表和按钮的列表对话框；
      </li>
      <li>
       带复选列表和按钮的列表对话框；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰AlertDialog提示对话框需要用AlertDialog.Builder来创建
      <br/>
      <strong>
       AlertDialog.Builder 的常用方法及功能
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         create()
        </td>
        <td>
         创建对话框
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setIcon(Drawable icon)
        </td>
        <td>
         为对话框设置图标
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setTitle(DharSequence title)
        </td>
        <td>
         为对话框设置标题
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setItems(CharSequence[] items, DialogInterface.OnClickListener listener )
        </td>
        <td>
         设置对话框显示的列表项
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setMessage(CharSequence message)
        </td>
        <td>
         为对话框设置消息内容
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setNegativeButton(CharSequence text, DialogInterface.OnClickListener listener )
        </td>
        <td>
         给对话框添加”取消“按钮
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setNeutralButton(CharSequence text, DialogInterface.OnClickListener listener )
        </td>
        <td>
         给对话框添加”中立“按钮
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setPositiveButton(CharSequence text, DialogInterface.OnClickListener listener )
        </td>
        <td>
         给对话框添加”确定“按钮
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setMultiChoiceItems(CharSequence[] items, boolean[] checkdItems, DIalogInterface.OnMultiChoiceClickListener listener)
        </td>
        <td>
         设置对话框显示的复选列表项
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setSingleChoiceItems(CharSequence[] items, int checkedItem, DialogInterface.OnClickListener listener)
        </td>
        <td>
         设置对话框显示的单选列表项
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         setView(View view)
        </td>
        <td>
         为对话框设置自定义样式
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         show()
        </td>
        <td>
         显示对话框
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔰创建对话框通常直接在Java代码中实现，不需要设计创建界面布局，通常由以下五个步骤：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       创建AlertDialog.Builder对象；
      </li>
      <li>
       调用setIcon()、setTitle()或setCustomTitle()等设置对话框标题栏的图标、标题等；
      </li>
      <li>
       调用setMessage()方法设置对话框中显示的消息内容或调用setItems()、setSingleChoiceItems()、setMultiChoiceItems()方法设置不同类别的对话框；
      </li>
      <li>
       调用setPositive/Negative/NeutralButton()方法设置确定、取消或中立按钮；
      </li>
      <li>
       调用create()、show()方法创建对话框对象并显示出来。
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_1200">
     </a>
     1）带消息和按钮的提示对话框
    </h5>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/de823f61ed182187722ea5f608281c7b.png"/>
      <br/>
      🔰创建对话框通常直接在Java代码中实现，不需要设计创建界面布局;
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">AlertDialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Builder</span> allertDang <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">AlertDialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Builder</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token comment">// 创建</span>
allertDang<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setTitle</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"课程评价调度"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">//设置标题</span>
allertDang<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"你喜欢这门课吗？"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">//设置显示信息</span>
allertDang<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setIcon</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ic_launcher<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token comment">//设置图标</span>

    <h5>
     <a id="5_1283">

     5）自定义对话框

     <p>

      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">LayoutInflater</span> layoutInflater <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token class-name">LayoutInflater</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">from</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <h5>
     <a id="6_1309">
     </a>
     6）提示对话框一般运用方式
    </h5>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/627168541b2b69402210319a9eb8bc1d.png"/>
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_ProgressDialog_1311">
     </a>
     2. ProgressDialog(进度条对话框)
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰ProgressDialog(进度条对话框)类继承自AlertDialog，它和ProgressBar(进度条)有着异曲同工之处，都是用于显示执行进度；不同的是
      <mark>
       ProgressDialog以对话框的形式展示出来
      </mark>
      。
      <br/>
      🔰ProgressDialog对话框进度的改变同样与ProgressBar一样，也需要使用线程来控制。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_1315">
     </a>
     1）进度条对话框创建
    </h5>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      1.直接采用new ProgressDialog( )创建
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span> dialog <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
dialog<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">//调用ProgressDialog的静态方法show( )创建并显示，此种方法只能创建默认的圆形条样式。</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/61ed015a17e8f58888ef76058b03e13c.png"/>
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span> dialog <span class="token operator">=</span>  <span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"提示"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">"正在登陆中"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">// /只能是圆形条，可以通过show()方法的参数设置title和Message提示内容。</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/4c80ffd095c6ff5413e47582adb95709.png"/>
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span> dialog2<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"提示"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"正在登录中"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> 
<span class="token comment">//使用静态方式创建并显示，只能是圆形条，最后一个参数boolean型，用于设置是否是不明确的状态。</span>

<span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span> dialog3<span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token class-name">ProgressDialog</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"提示"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"正在登录中"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token comment">//使用静态方式创建并显示，只能是圆形条，最后一个参数boolean型，用于设置是否进度条是可以取消的。</span>
</code></pre>

    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="__1426">
     </a>
     六. 服务和消息广播
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Service_1427">
     </a>
     (一) Service
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_Service_1428">
     </a>
     1. Service简介
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Service是Android的四大组件之一，没有用户界面、不能直接与用户交互、通常在后台执行耗时操作的应用组件。
      <br/>
      🔰主要用途有两个：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       后台运行：通过启动一个服务，可以在不显示界面的情况下在后台运行指定的任务，这样可以不影响用户做其他事情。
      </li>
      <li>
       跨进程访问：通过 AIDL （ Android InterfaceDefinition Language）可以实现在不同进程之间的通信。
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_Service_1433">
     </a>
     2. Service生命周期
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Service的启动和关闭有以下两种方式：
      <br/>
      🔹1. 启动式：通过
      <mark>
       其他组件调用 startService() 方法启动Service
      </mark>
      ，通过
      <mark>
       其他组件调用stopService()方法或Service本身调用stopSelf()方法关闭Service
      </mark>
      。当Service被停止时，系统会销毁它，这种方式调用简单，控制方便。
      <br/>
      》🔹但
      <mark>
       一旦启动了Service，除了再次调用或关闭Service外就再没有办法对Service内部状态进行操作控制
      </mark>
      ，缺乏灵活性。也就是说通过该方式启动的Service与启动它的组件没有关联，
      <strong>
       既使启动它的组件退出了，Service也仍然在后台运行
      </strong>
      。
      <br/>
      🔹2. 绑定式：通过
      <mark>
       其他组件(客户)调用bindService()方法启动Service，其他组件(客户)可以通过一个IBinder接口与Service进行通信，也可以通过调用unbindService()方法关闭Service
      </mark>
      。
      <br/>
      》🔹这种方式
      <mark>
       可以通过IBinder接口获取Service，对Service状态进行检测
      </mark>
      。即通过该方式启动的Service与启动它的组件(客户)绑定在一起，
      <strong>
       组件(客户)一旦退出，Service也随之关闭
      </strong>
      。
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/8bda4f1f148efc019079d67ba0d12573.png"/>
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      开启获取电话状态权限:
      <br/>
      <code>
       &lt;uses-permission android:name="android.permission.READ_PHONE_STATE"/&gt;
      </code>
      <br/>
      开启录音权限:
      <br/>
      <code>
       &lt;uses-permission android:name="android.permission.RECORD_AUDIO"/&gt;
      </code>
      <br/>
      开启SD卡写入权限:
      <br/>
      <code>
       &lt;uses-permission android:name="android.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE" /&gt;
      </code>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="3__1448">
     </a>
     3. 设置服务
    </h4>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/3a7955d59639846fd840c1f5e481b81e.png"/>
    </p>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_BroadcastReceiver_1453">
     </a>
     (二) BroadcastReceiver
    </h3>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_BroadcastReceiver_1454">
     </a>
     1. BroadcastReceiver简介
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰BroadcastReceiver也是Android的四大组件之一，通常一旦产生某个事件时就可以发送一个广播，应用程序使用BroadcastReceiver接收广播后就会知道系统产生了什么事件，同时也可以根据相应的事件作出相应的处理。
      <br/>
      🔰BroadcastReceiver本质上可以认为就是一个监听器，但是
      <strong>
       通常的监听器是程序级别的，当程序退出时监听器也会随之关闭
      </strong>
      ；
      <mark>
       BroadcastReceiver是系统级别的监听器，只要与该监听器匹配的Intent被广播出来，BroadcastReceiver就会被激发并根据相应的操作进行处理
      </mark>
      。
      <br/>
      🔰BroadcastReceiver有两种类型：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       普通广播：无序广播，
       <mark>
        可以同一时间被所有与广播Intent匹配的接收者同时接收，接收者之间相互不会有影响
       </mark>
       。
      </li>
      <li>
       有序广播：按照一定优先级进行消息的接收，
       <mark>
        首先发送到与广播Intent匹配的优先级最高的接收者那里，然后再从前面的接收者传播到下一个优先级的接收者那里。优先级高的接收者也可以终止这个广播
       </mark>
       。优先级取值可通过-1000~1000，数值越大，优先级越高。
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_BroadcastReceiver_1461">
     </a>
     2. BroadcastReceiver生命周期
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰每次广播到来时 ， 会重新创建BroadcastReceiver 对象，并且调用 onReceive() 方法 ，执行完以后 , 该对象即被销毁。
      <br/>
      🔰 onReceive() 方法在 10 秒内没有执行完毕， Android 会认为该程序无响应 。所以在BroadcastReceiver 里不能做一些比较耗时的操作，否侧会弹出 ANR(Application NoResponse) 的对话框。
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/5a1b146c46f5b2ea8a562b882948d8c9.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_AlarmManager_1467">
     </a>
     (三) AlarmManager
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Android系统中有一个AlarmManager的对应服务程序——AlarmManagerServie，该服务程序用于提供闹铃服务，它主要
      <mark>
       维护应用程序注册下来的各类闹铃并适时地设置即将触发的闹铃给闹铃设备，并且一直监听闹铃设备
      </mark>
      ，一旦有闹铃触发或者是闹铃事件发生，AlarmManagerServie就会遍历闹铃列表找到相应的注册闹铃并发出广播。
      <br/>
      🔰
      <strong>
       AlarmManager的主要方法：
      </strong>
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/6526e375d3b62fe1b5047f90270bd341.png"/>
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Alarm的type主要类型：
      </strong>
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/0aad2ebd0d288ecb94f9e6c1a55065cc.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="__1479">
     </a>
     七. 数据的存储与访问
    </h2>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰各类应用开发中，数据存储访问方式有三类：文件、数据库和网络(云存储)。
      <br/>
      🔰Android存储方式总体也分为以上三类，包含以下五种：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       SharedPreference存储访问机制
       <br/>
       <em>
        存储简单配置信息，只能存储Long、Float、Integer、String和Boolean五种，以键值存储在XML中；
       </em>
      </li>
      <li>
       文件存储访问机制
       <br/>
       <em>
        采用java.io.*库提供的I/O接口实现文件读写，需在res/目录下适当子目录创建和存储；
       </em>
      </li>
      <li>
       SQLite数据库数据存储访问机制
       <br/>
       <em>
        轻量级嵌入式数据库引擎，支持SQL语言，并占用较少存；
       </em>
      </li>
      <li>
       ContentProvider共享数据机制
       <br/>
       <em>
        提供标准方法接口，实其他应用保存和读取ContentProvider各种数；
       </em>
      </li>
      <li>
       网络数据存储访问机制
       <br/>
       <em>
        Android网络存储使用HTTP协议，采用J2SE包。
       </em>
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰五种方式各有优缺点，根据实际开发情况选择。数据较少时，建议使用SharedPreference；数据量较大时，可选择文件或数据库存储。
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Android平台设备的存储器，包括内存、内部存储器和外部存储器：
      </strong>
      <br/>
      🔹
      <mark>
       内存
      </mark>
      即Memory，当系统运行和App运行时必须将程序的核心模块加载到内存中；
      <br/>
      🔹
      <mark>
       内部存储器
      </mark>
      即InternalStorage，它的空间十分有限，是Android系统本身和系统应用程序主要的数据存储所在位置，一旦内部存储空间耗尽，Android平台设备也就无法使用了，
      <em>
       开发者应该尽量避免在编码时使用内部存储空间
      </em>
      ；
      <br/>
      🔹
      <mark>
       外部存储器
      </mark>
      即ExternalStorage，它和SD卡没有必然的联系，通常包含公有目录和私有目录两类子文件夹。
     </p>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Android系统的目录结构中有三个重要的文件夹：
      </strong>
      <br/>
      🔹data文件夹：即内部存储器对应的文件夹，存放所有安装的App文件；
      <br/>
      🔹storage文件夹：即外部存储器对应的文件夹，不同设备不同，一般该文件夹内有一个sdcard文件夹。
      <br/>
      🔹mnt文件夹：同storage文件夹。因内存空间有限，Google建议将App数据存储在外部存储器该目录下。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_SharedPreferences_1504">
     </a>
     (一) SharedPreferences存储访问机制
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       SharedPreferences的常用方法
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         boolean contains(String key)
        </td>
        <td>
         判断SharedPreferences是否包含特定key的数据
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         SharedPreferences.Editor edit()
        </td>
        <td>
         返回一个Edit对象用于操作SharedPreferences
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         Map&lt;String, ?&gt;getAll()
        </td>
        <td>
         获取SharedPreferences数据里全部的key-value对
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         getXXX(String key, XXX defValue)
        </td>
        <td>
         获取SharedPreferences数据指定key所对应的value， 如果该key不存在，返回默认值defValue。其中XXX可以是Boolean， float， int， long， String等基本类型 的值
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Editor的常用方法
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         SharedPreferences.Editor clear()
        </td>
        <td>
         清除SharedPreferences里所有的数据
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         boolean commit()
        </td>
        <td>
         当Editor编辑完成后，调用该方法可以提交修改，而且必须要调用这个方法数据才能修改
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         SharedPreferences.Editor putXXX(String key, boolean XXX)
        </td>
        <td>
         向SharedPreferences存入指定的key对应的数据。其中XXX可以是是Boolean， float， int， long， String等基本类型 的值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         SharedPreferences.Editor remove(String key)
        </td>
        <td>
         删除SharedPreferences里指定的key对应的数据项
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      <strong>
       🔰SharedPreferences
       <mark>
        存储数据
       </mark>
       四个步骤：
      </strong>
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       获取SharedPreferences对象
       <br/>
       通过Context类中的getSharedPreferences(String name,int mode)方法，它的操作权限属于整个应用程序，每个Activity可以对应多个xml存储文件，由第一个参数name为文件名保存在系统中(名称不需要带后缀xml，保存文件时系统自动加后缀)，第二个参数mode表示文件的操作模式，其值及功能如表所示。
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">SharedPreferences</span> sp <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">getSharedPreferences</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginconfig"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Context</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>MODE_PRIVATE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      <strong>
       文件操作模式及功能
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         Context.MODE_PRIVATE
        </td>
        <td>
         为默认操作模式，代表该文件是私有数据，只能应用程序本身使用，在该模式下，写入的内容会覆盖原文件的内容。
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         Context.MODE_APPEND
        </td>
        <td>
         该模式会检查文件是否存在，如果存在就向文件中追加内容，否则就创建新文件
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         Context.MODE_WORLD_READABLE
        </td>
        <td>
         表示当前文件可以被其他应用程序读取
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         Context.MODE_WORLD_WRITEABLE
        </td>
        <td>
         表示当前文件可以被其他应用程序写入
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <ol start="2">
      <li>
       通过SharedPreferences对象的edit()方法获得SharedPreferences.Editor对象；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">SharedPreferences<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Editor</span> editor <span class="token operator">=</span> sp<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">edit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="3">
      <li>
       通过Editor对象的putXXX()方法，将不同类型的数据以key-value键值对的形式存储；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">editor<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginname"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> username<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token comment">//用户名</span>
editor<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginpwd"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> password<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token comment">//密码</span>
editor<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putBoolean</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginsave"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> issave<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token comment">//保存密码</span>
editor<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">putBoolean</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginauto"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> isauto<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token comment">//自动登录</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="4">
      <li>
       完成以上步骤后，此时的数据仍然在内存中，需要通过Editor对象的commit()方法提交数据，也就是将数据保存到xml文件中。
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">editor<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">commit</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      <strong>
       🔰SharedPreferences
       <mark>
        读取数据
       </mark>
       四个步骤：
      </strong>
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       获取SharedPreferences对象实例:(与存储相同)
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">SharedPreferences</span> sp <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">getSharedPreferences</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginconfig"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Context</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>MODE_PRIVATE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="2">
      <li>
       读取数据：
       <br/>
       1）读取单一数据时，利用getString()方法,读取已经保存
       <br/>
       在文件中的用户名和密码；
       <br/>
       <code>
        String uname = sp.getString("username", "admin"); // 当不能读出时，默认值为admin
       </code>
       <br/>
       2）读取全部数据时，利用getAll()方法,再遍历map；
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token class-name">Map</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> <span class="token function">reads</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token class-name">SharedPreferences</span> sp <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">getSharedPreferences</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginconfig"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Context</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>MODE_PRIVATE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token class-name">String</span> content <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token string">""</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token class-name">Map</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> allContent <span class="token operator">=</span> sp<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getAll</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token keyword">for</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Map<span class="token punctuation">.</span>Entry</span><span class="token generics"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">String</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token operator">?</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span> entry<span class="token operator">:</span> allContent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">entrySet</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
		content <span class="token operator">+=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>entry<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getKey</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">+</span> entry<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
	<span class="token keyword">return</span> content<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="3">
      <li>
       定义read()方法，读出数据：
      </li>
     </ol>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">read</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token class-name">SharedPreferences</span> sp <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">getSharedPreferences</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"DengLu"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">Context</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>MODE_PRIVATE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token class-name">String</span> uname <span class="token operator">=</span> sp<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginname"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">""</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token class-name">String</span> upwd <span class="token operator">=</span> sp<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginpwd"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">""</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token keyword">boolean</span> jizhu1 <span class="token operator">=</span> sp<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getBoolean</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginsave"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token keyword">boolean</span> zidong1 <span class="token operator">=</span> sp<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getBoolean</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"loginauto"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
	<span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>jizhu1<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token comment">//如果前次登录选择了保存密码， 则将用户名和密码读出后，显示在对应位置</span>
		zhanghao<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>uname<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
		mima<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>upwd<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
	<span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>zidong1<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token comment">//如果前次选择了自动登录， 则开启程序后直接跳转到InfoActivity</span>
		<span class="token class-name">Intent</span> intent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Intent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token class-name">InfoActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">class</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
		<span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">startActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>intent<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
     <ol start="4">
      <li>
       onCreate()方法中初始化对象：
       <br/>
       <a href="https://blog.csdn.net/qq_51712954/article/details/123770213?csdn_share_tail=%7B%22type%22:%22blog%22,%22rType%22:%22article%22,%22rId%22:%22123770213%22,%22source%22:%22qq_51712954%22%7D">
        SharedPreferences存储访问机制
       </a>
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1588">
     </a>
     (二) 文件存储访问机制
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <mark>
       Java提供了一套完整的IO流体系用来对文件进行操作
      </mark>
      ，包括FileInputStream、FileOutputStream等，通过这些IO流可以非常方便地访问磁盘上的文件。
      <br/>
      🔰
      <mark>
       Android同样支持以流的方式来访问Android平台设备存储上的文件
      </mark>
      ，包括设备本身的存储设备(内部存储器，InternalStorage)或外接的存储设备(外部存储器，ExternalStorage)。
      <br/>
      🔰另 外
      <mark>
       Android中 的Context类对象提供了openFileOutput()、openFileInput()两个方法分别获得输入流和输出流，从而实现文件的读写操作
      </mark>
      。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_Java_IO_1592">
     </a>
     1. Java IO流
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰File类以及FileInputStream、FileOutputStream、FileReader及FileWriter处理字节流和字符流。
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         方法
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File(FIle dir, String name)
        </td>
        <td>
         dir 为FIle 对象类型的目标路径，name 为文件名或目录
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File(String path)
        </td>
        <td>
         path 为新File对象的路径
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File(String dirPath, String name)
        </td>
        <td>
         dirPath 为指定文件路径，name为文件名或目录名
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File(URI uri)
        </td>
        <td>
         使用URI指定路径创建新的FIle对象
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/2f413d79e46773072451062c10cd2519.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="2__1603">
     </a>
     2. 读写内部存储器的文件数据
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Android中Context类提供两种方法打开数据文件IO流：
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       <code>
        FileInputStream openFileInput(String name)
       </code>
       ：打开应用程序的数据文件下的name文件对应的输入流；
      </li>
      <li>
       <code>
        FileOutputStream openFileOutput(String name, int mode)
       </code>
       ：打开应用程序的数据文件下的name文件对应的输出流。
      </li>
     </ol>
     <p>
      🔰另外Context类还提供下表所示的常用方法。这些方法都是通过上下文对象Context获取的，新创建的文件和目录都属于本应用程序所有。只要应用程序被卸载，这些文件或目录都会被清空。
      <br/>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Context类与文件操作有关的方法
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File getFilesDir()
        </td>
        <td>
         返回本应用程序的数据文件夹的绝对路径。在这里获取到的是”/data/data/&lt;包名&gt;/files/"目录，返回File对象
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File getCacheDir()
        </td>
        <td>
         返回本应用程序默认的缓存文件存放路径。用于获取”/data/data/&lt;包名&gt;/cache/“目录，返回File对象
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File getExternalCacheDir()
        </td>
        <td>
         返回本应用程序在外部存储的存储目录。用于获取"/cache/"目录， 返回File对象
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String[] fileList()
        </td>
        <td>
         返回本应用程序的数据文件夹的全部文件
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         Boolean deleteFile(String)
        </td>
        <td>
         删除本应用程序的数据文件夹下的指定文件
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File getDatabasePath(String name)
        </td>
        <td>
         返回以openOrCreateDatabase(String, int, SQLiteDatabase.CursorFactory)方法创建的数据库的绝对路径
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         File getFileStreamPath(String name)
        </td>
        <td>
         返回以openFileOutput(String , int)方法创建的文件的绝对路径
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      <a href="https://blog.csdn.net/qq_51712954/article/details/123770213?csdn_share_tail=%7B%22type%22:%22blog%22,%22rType%22:%22article%22,%22rId%22:%22123770213%22,%22source%22:%22qq_51712954%22%7D">
       文件存储访问机制——读写内部存储器
      </a>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="3__1622">
     </a>
     3. 读写外部存储器的文件数据
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Android应用开发中
      <mark>
       常使用Environment类获取外部存储器目录
      </mark>
      。在访问外部存储器之前一定要先判断外部存储器是否已经是可使用状态（即已挂载或可使用），并且需要在AndroidManifest.xml配置文件中添加外部存储读和写的权限。
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 在SD卡中创建与删除文件的权限 --&gt;</span> 
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>uses-permission</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>android.permission.MOUNT_UNMOUNT_FILESYSTEMS<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
<span class="token comment">&lt;!-- 向SD卡中写入数据的权限 --&gt;</span> 
<span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>uses-permission</span> <span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>android.permission.WRITE_EXTERNAL_STORAGE<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       外部存储状态表示
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         静态常量
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_BAD_REMOVAL
        </td>
        <td>
         在没有挂载前存储媒体已经被移除
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_CHECKING
        </td>
        <td>
         正在检查存储媒体
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_MOUNTED
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体已经挂载，并且挂载点可读写
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_MOUNTED_READ_ONLY
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体已经挂载，挂载点只读
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_NOFS
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体是空白或是不支持的文件系统
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_REMOVED
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体被移除
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_SHARED
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体正在通过USB共享
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_UNMOUNTABLE
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体无法挂载
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         String MEDIA_UNMOUNTED
        </td>
        <td>
         存储媒体没有挂载
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       系统其他标准目录
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>

     <hr/>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Environment类的常用方法
      </strong>
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th align="left">
         方法名
        </th>
        <th>
         功能说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         FIle getDataDirectory()
        </td>

        </td>

        </td>

        </td>

         获取外部存储媒体目录
        </td>

        </td>
        <td>
         获取特定类型文件的上一级外部存储目录
        </td>
       </tr>

        <td align="left">
         String getExternalStorageState()
        </td>
        <td>
         获取当前外部储存媒体的状态
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">

        </td>

        </td>

        </td>

        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>

         static boolean isExternalStorageEmulated(File path)
        </td>
        <td>
         判断指定文件目录的外部存储媒体是否是内存模拟的，是则返回true
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         static boolean isExternalStorageRemovable()
        </td>
        <td>
         判断设备的外存是否可拆卸，如SD卡，是则返回true
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td align="left">
         static boolean isExternalStorageRemovable(File path)
        </td>
        <td>
         判断指定目录下的外存是否可拆卸，如SD卡，是则返回true
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔹 第1步：AndroidMainFest.xml中添加读写SD卡权限；
      <br/>
      🔹第2步：判断Android设备上是否已插入SD卡:
      <br/>
      <code>
       Environment.getExternalStorageState().equals(Environment.MEDIA_MOUNTED);
      </code>
      <br/>
      🔹第3步：调用Environment.getExternalStorageDirectory()获得SD卡根目录；
      <br/>
      <code>
       File SDCardRoot=Environment.getExternalStorageDirectory();
      </code>
      <br/>
      🔹第4步：读写SD卡中的文件；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="4__1679">
     </a>
     4. 读写资源文件数据
    </h4>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       Android系统的资源文件可以分为两种：
      </strong>
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       第一种是res/raw目录下的资源文件，这类资源文件会在R.java里面自动生成该资源文件的ID；
      </li>
      <li>
       第二种是assets目录下存放的原生资源文件，它不会被映射到R.java文件中，所以不能通过R.XXX.ID的方式访问。
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_res_1683">
     </a>
     1) res目录下的资源文件
    </h5>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰要在res目录下放置数据文件，通常需要手动在该目录下创建raw目录，然后把数据文件复制到该目录下。
      <br/>
      🔰例如下面代码表示读出raw目录下的test文件。
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/19c357038ecde14735b9708b7d0947f5.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h5>
     <a id="2_assets_1686">
     </a>
     2) assets目录下的资源文件
    </h5>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰使用Android Studio创建项目时，开发环境不会自动创建assets目录，如果开发者需要使用这个文件夹存储原生资源文件，就需要在项目的res/main文件下手动创建assets文件夹，创建完成后将需要使用的原生资源文件复制到该文件夹中即可。
      <br/>
      🔰例如下面代码表示定义一个方法读出assets目录下的fileName文件。
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/4f64c7fbde11ae1a1cee6e354e206c76.png"/>
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="_SQLite_1695">
     </a>
     (三) SQLite数据库数据存储访问机制
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <mark>
       轻量级嵌入式数据库引擎，支持SQL语言，并占用较少存；
      </mark>
      <br/>
      🔰SQLite数据库系统采用的是动态数据类型，使用时会根据存入的具体值自动判断其数据类型。
      <br/>
      🔰通常SQLite包含NULL、INTEGER(整数)、REAL( 浮点数 ) 、 TEXT( 字符串文本 ) 和BLOB(二进制对象)五种数据类型，因为其采用动态数据类型，所以对于varchar、char等其他数据类型也同样可以保存。比如可以在INTEGER类型的字段中存放字符串类型。
      <br/>
      🔰SQLite通过文件来保存数据库，一个文件就是一个数据库，一个数据库中可以包含多个表，每个表里又可以有多条记录，每条记录又由多个字段构成，每个字段可以指定其数据类型(主键对应的字段必须指定数据类型)和对应的值。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__1700">
     </a>
     1. 手动创建数据库的两种途径
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1_CMD_1701">
     </a>
     1) 直接在CMD命令窗口中手动创建
    </h5>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ContentProvider_1703">
     </a>
     (四) ContentProvider共享数据机制
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰提供标准方法接口，实其他应用保存和读取ContentProvider各种数；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1705">
     </a>
     (五) 网络数据存储访问机制
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Android网络存储使用HTTP协议，采用J2SE包。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="__1709">
     </a>
     八. 多媒体应用开发
    </h2>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰Android的多媒体核心框架是OpenCore，兼顾了跨平台的移植性，也有较好的稳定性；
      <br/>
      🔰主要包含两大方面：PVPlayer(媒体播放)和PVAuthor(媒体记录)，并以SDK的形式提供给开发者；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <hr/>
    <h2>
     <a id="_1721">
     </a>
     常用功能类
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_Toast_1722">
     </a>
     (一) 消息提示框机制【Toast】
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰
      <strong>
       可以在用户做了某种操作后，给用户一些提示消息。该提示信息不能被用户操作，提示后自动消失；
      </strong>
      <br/>
      效果如下：
      <br/>
      <code>
       Toast.makeText(this,"成功",Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show();
      </code>
      <br/>
      <code>
       this
      </code>
      ：为当前activity；
      <br/>
      <code>
       "成功"
      </code>
      ：为要显示的字符串；
      <br/>
      <code>
       Toast.LENGTH_LONG
      </code>
      ：为内容显示的时间，也可以自定义；
      <br/>
      <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/30adbf01455a0bdc07b69a70455258b2.png"/>
      <br/>
      🔰创建并显示Toast有两种方式：
      <br/>
      1) 默认Toast：
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">	 btnLogin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Button</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>btnLogin<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
     btnLogin<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">View<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
           <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
           <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> sUserName<span class="token operator">=</span>edtUserName<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> sPWD<span class="token operator">=</span>edtPWD<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token keyword">if</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sUserName<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">equals</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"2021"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span>sPWD<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">equals</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"2021"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
               <span class="token comment">//默认Toast</span>
                   <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">makeText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"登录成功"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_LONG<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                   <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">makeText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"QQ号或密码错误，请重新输入！"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_LONG<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
          <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
     <p>
      2) 自定义Toast：(显示图片)
     </p>
     <pre><code class="prism language-java">	   btnLogin <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Button</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>btnLogin<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
       btnLogin<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">View<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnClickListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
           <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
           <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onClick</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">View</span> v<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> sUserName<span class="token operator">=</span>edtUserName<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token class-name">String</span> sPWD<span class="token operator">=</span>edtPWD<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token keyword">if</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>sUserName<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">equals</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"2021"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span>sPWD<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">equals</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">"2021"</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                   <span class="token comment">//定义Toast</span>
                   <span class="token class-name">Toast</span> toast <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//定义一个ImageView</span>
                   <span class="token class-name">ImageView</span> imageView <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">ImageView</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//定义显示的图片</span>
                   imageView<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setImageResource</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>drawable<span class="token punctuation">.</span>ic_launcher_background<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//定义一个LinearLayou，也可以是其他的布局</span>
                   <span class="token class-name">LinearLayout</span> layout <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">LinearLayout</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//布局显示方式</span>
                   layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOrientation</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">LinearLayout</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>HORIZONTAL<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//将ImageView放到layout中</span>
                   layout<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">addView</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>imageView<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//设置view</span>
                   toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setView</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>layout<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   <span class="token comment">//设置显示时间</span>
                   toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setDuration</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_LONG<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                   toast<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                   <span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">makeText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token string">"QQ号或密码错误，请重新输入！"</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span><span class="token class-name">Toast</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>LENGTH_LONG<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">show</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
               <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
           <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
       <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_CountDownTimer_1780">
     </a>
     (二) 倒计时函数【CountDownTimer】
    </h3>
    <p>
     <strong>
      CountDownTimer的常用方法和功能说明
     </strong>
    </p>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        方法名
       </th>
       <th>
        功能说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        CountDownTimer(long time, long interval)
       </td>
       <td>
        构造方法，time表示从开始调用到start()到倒计时完成并调用onFinish()方法的总时间；
        <br/>
        interval表示调用onTick()方法的间隔时间，单位为毫秒
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        cancel()
       </td>
       <td>
        取消倒计时
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        onFinsih()
       </td>
       <td>
        抽象方法，倒计时完成被调用
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        start()
       </td>
       <td>
        倒计时开始
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        onTick(longtime)
       </td>
       <td>
        抽象方法，每个间隔时间interval一到就会调用一次，time表示剩余时间
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      <strong>
       倒计时器的实现
      </strong>
     </p>
     <ol>
      <li>
       创建一个继承CountDownTimer的内部类MyCount,并重写方法
      </li>
      <li>
       给按钮设置监听事件
       <br/>
       <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/3f194ed91d8d1ce363ce7d55ddda2303.png"/>
       <br/>
       具体实现及效果看
       <a href="https://blog.csdn.net/qq_51712954/article/details/123770213?spm=1001.2014.3001.5501">
        【移动应用开发实践案列】
       </a>
      </li>
     </ol>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1797">
     </a>
     (三) 消息处理机制
    </h3>
    <p>
     🔰案例：输入数字，计时到等于输入数字
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">class</span> <span class="token class-name">MainActivity</span> <span class="token keyword">extends</span> <span class="token class-name">AppCompatActivity</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token class-name">TextView</span> tv<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <span class="token keyword">int</span> i <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token comment">// 创建Handler对象用于处理消息</span>
    <span class="token class-name">Handler</span> handler <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Handler</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
        <span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">handleMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Message</span> msg<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
            <span class="token keyword">super</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">handleMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>msg<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
            tv<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>msg<span class="token punctuation">.</span>arg1<span class="token operator">+</span><span class="token string">""</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
        <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token comment">// 创建Runnable用于在子线程中实现功能需求</span>
    <span class="token class-name">Runnable</span> runnable <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Runnable</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>

        	<span class="token comment">// 判断输入数字是否等于i</span>
        	<span class="token comment">// Integer.parseInt(edit.getText().toString()) 获取输入的数字，转换成int类型</span>
            <span class="token keyword">while</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>i<span class="token operator">&lt;=</span> <span class="token class-name">Integer</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">parseInt</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>edit<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getText</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">toString</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> 
                <span class="token class-name">Message</span> msg <span class="token operator">=</span> handler<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">obtainMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                msg<span class="token punctuation">.</span>arg1<span class="token operator">=</span>i<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                handler<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">sendMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>msg<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                    <span class="token class-name">Thread</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">sleep</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token number">1000</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
                <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">InterruptedException</span> e<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
                    e<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">printStackTrace</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
                i<span class="token operator">++</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
    <span class="token keyword">protected</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCreate</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Bundle</span> savedInstanceState<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1845">
     </a>
     (四) 横竖屏设置
    </h3>
    <p>
     <strong>
      1.AndroidMainfest.xml中修改screenOrientation属性：
     </strong>
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-xml"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>activity</span>
	<span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>name</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>.MainActivity<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span>
	<span class="token attr-name"><span class="token namespace">android:</span>screenOrientation</span><span class="token attr-value"><span class="token punctuation attr-equals">=</span><span class="token punctuation">"</span>landscape<span class="token punctuation">"</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>activity</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</code></pre>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        属性值
       </th>
       <th>
        说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        unspecified
       </td>
       <td>
        默认值，由系统根据设备来判断显示方向
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        landscape
       </td>
       <td>
        横屏显示
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        portrait
       </td>
       <td>
        竖屏显示
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        user
       </td>
       <td>
        用户当前首先的方向
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        begind
       </td>
       <td>
        和该 Activity 下面的那个 Activity 的方向一致(在 Activity 堆栈中的)
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        sensor
       </td>
       <td>
        有物理感应器来决定，用户旋转设备会导致屏幕的横竖屏切换
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        nosensor
       </td>
       <td>
        忽略物理感应器，用户旋转设备不会导致屏幕的横竖屏切换
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p>
     <strong>
      2. MainActivity.java中用功能代码实现：
     </strong>
     <br/>
     🔷在需要横屏显示的Activity中的Oncreate()方法中增加如下代码：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token function">setRequestedOrientation</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">Activitylnfo</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>SCREEN_ORIENTATION_LANDSCAPE<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1870">
     </a>
     (五) 滚动视图设置
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔷
      <mark>
       HorizontalScrollView(水平滚动视图)布局容器，使用它可以实现左右+
       <br/>
       滚动来显示内容；
      </mark>
      <br/>
      🔷
      <mark>
       ScrollView(垂直滚视图)布局容器，使用它可以实现上下滚动来显示内容；
      </mark>
      <br/>
      🔷HorizontalScrollView和ScrollView都是FrameLayout的子类，它们的使用方法一样；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="_ProgressBar_1876">
     </a>
     (六) ProgressBar进度条
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔷提示用户后台App的执行进度，提高界面友好性；
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性 / 方法
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android: max
        </td>
        <td>
         设置进度条的最大值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android: progress
        </td>
        <td>
         设置当前第一进度值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         android:secondaryProgress
        </td>
        <td>
         设置当前第二进度值设置是否显示
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         synchronized int getMax()
        </td>
        <td>
         获取进度条的最大值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         synchronized int getProgress()
        </td>
        <td>
         获取当前第一进度值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         synchronized int getSecondaryProgress()
        </td>
        <td>
         获取当前第二进度值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         synchronized void setMax(int max)
        </td>
        <td>
         设置进度条的最大值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         synchronized void setProgress(int progress)
        </td>
        <td>
         设置第一进度值
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         synchronized void setSecondaryProgress(int secondaryProgress)
        </td>
        <td>
         设置第二进度值
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
     <p>
      🔷Android系统中内置了多种不同风格的进度条，在布局文件中通过style属性值来设置ProgressBar的风格；
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔷系统内置了多种不同风格的进度条，在布局中通过style属性来设置。style属性属性值如下：
     </p>
     <table>
      <thead>
       <tr>
        <th>
         属性值
        </th>
        <th>
         说明
        </th>
       </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
       <tr>
        <td>
         style=‘@style/Widget.AppCompat.ProgressBar.Horizontal’
        </td>
        <td>
         <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/b0bcfca959b9794f4fa77e6c3d69f44e.png"/>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         style=‘@style/Widget.AppCompat.ProgressBar’
        </td>
        <td>
         <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/fcaa280af9190e019f69d5b1e752cf3a.png"/>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         style=‘@android:style/Widget.ProgressBar.Horizontal’
        </td>
        <td>
         <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/38d56898402aa37f8572dcf7f8a89209.png"/>
        </td>
       </tr>
       <tr>
        <td>
         style=‘@android:style/Widget.ProgressBar.Inverse’
        </td>

         <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/d6e356b60a69d24fa8e19e3ddf076266.png"/>
        </td>
       </tr>
      </tbody>
     </table>
    </blockquote>
    <hr/>
    <h3>
     <a id="__1900">
     </a>
     (七) 开关
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      🔰ToggleButton开关按钮，Switch开关，两个组件都是继承自CompoundButton。
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <h4>
     <a id="1_ToggleButton_1902">
     </a>
     1. 开关按钮【ToggleButton】
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        属性
       </th>
       <th>
        说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:disabledAlpha=“0.5”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置按钮禁用时的透明度
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:textOff=“关闭”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置按钮没有被选中时显示的文字
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:textOn=“开启”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置按钮被选中时显示的文字
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/d71cf6854978816ffb82adac75a88c57.png"/>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/e2780abb45bd4c759a4a59abbc696e8d.png"/>
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="2_Switch_1912">
     </a>
     2. Switch开关
    </h4>
    <table>
     <thead>
      <tr>
       <th>
        属性
       </th>
       <th>
        说明
       </th>
      </tr>
     </thead>
     <tbody>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:showText=“false”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置on/off 的时候是否显示文字
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:splitTrack=“false”
       </td>
       <td>
        是否设置一个间隙，让滑块与底部图片分隔
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:switchPadding=“2dp”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置滑块内文字的间隔
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:switchMinWidth=“20dp”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置开关的最小宽度
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:track=“@mipmap/tupian”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置开关背景图片
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        android:thumb=“@mipmap/tupian”
       </td>
       <td>
        设置开关滑块图片
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/3082d5e3300b5421c40f49130d3011be.png"/>
     <img alt="在这里插入图片描述" src="https://i-blog.csdnimg.cn/blog_migrate/7b45d40661022086cd69af33926dcfd6.png"/>
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="3__1923">
     </a>
     3. 开关监听事件
    </h4>
    <pre><code class="prism language-java"><span class="token class-name">ImageView</span> img <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>img<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
<span class="token class-name">Switch</span> sw <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">findViewById</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">.</span>sw<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
sw<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setOnCheckedChangeListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">CompoundButton<span class="token punctuation">.</span>OnCheckedChangeListener</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
	<span class="token annotation punctuation">@Override</span>
	<span class="token keyword">public</span> <span class="token keyword">void</span> <span class="token function">onCheckedChanged</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">CompoundButton</span> compoundButton<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token keyword">boolean</span> b<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
		<span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>b<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
			img<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setImageResource</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>nanhai<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
		<span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
			img<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setImageResource</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token class-name">R</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>mipmap<span class="token punctuation">.</span>maozua<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
		<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
	<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</code></pre>
